002-2v-3a1 1 0 10-2 0v3H5V7h3a1 1 0 000-2H5z"></path></svg></a></div></div></div></div><p>This guide provides a deep dive into the key pieces that make Zag machines

<h2 id="machine-fundamentals" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Machine Fundamentals<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-fundamentals"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>A state machine is a way to model stateful, reactive behavior using:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">A finite number of states</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">A finite number of transitions between those states</li>
</ul>
<p>Before diving into context, computed values, refs, and effects, start with this
minimal toggle machine.</p>
<h3 id="create-a-machine" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Create a Machine<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#create-a-machine"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<p>The rest of this guide explains the advanced building blocks used in production
machines.</p>
<h2 id="nested-states" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Nested States<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#nested-states"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Machines can now model hierarchical state by nesting <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">states</code> inside a parent
state and defining the child&#x27;s <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initial</code> state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> createMachine <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/core&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> machine <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">createMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">initialState</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token string">&quot;closed&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  states<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    closed<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      on<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token constant">OPEN</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> target<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;open.idle&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    open<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      initial<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;idle&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      states<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        idle<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> on<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token constant">SUBMIT</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> target<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;open.submitting&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        submitting<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">          on<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">            <span class="token constant">SUCCESS</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> target<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;closed&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">            <span class="token constant">ERROR</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> target<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;open.idle&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">          <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      on<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token constant">CLOSE</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> target<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;closed&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Key points:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Use dot notation for nested targets, like <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open.submitting</code></li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Parent states can still define transitions (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open -&gt; CLOSE</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Check nested activity with <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">service.state.matches(&quot;open.idle&quot;)</code></li>
</ul>
<h2 id="context" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Context holds the reactive state of your machine. Unlike props (which are
configuration), context represents internal state that changes over time.</p>
<p>Context values are created using the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">bindable</code> pattern, which provides
controlled/uncontrolled state management.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token function">context</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> bindable<span class="token punctuation">,</span> prop <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Uncontrolled state with default value</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    count<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token generic-function"><span class="token function">bindable</span><span class="token generic class-name"><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token builtin">number</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span></span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      defaultValue<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Controlled/uncontrolled state</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token generic-function"><span class="token function">bindable</span><span class="token generic class-name"><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token builtin">string</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span></span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      defaultValue<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;defaultName&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">??</span> <span class="token string">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// When provided, state is controlled</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">onChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>value<span class="token punctuation">,</span> prev<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;onNameChange&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">?.</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> value <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="bindable-parameters" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Bindable Parameters<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#bindable-parameters"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code></strong>: Initial value for uncontrolled state</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code></strong>: Controlled value from props (when provided, state becomes
controlled)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onChange</code></strong>: Callback fired when value changes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isEqual</code></strong>: Custom equality function (defaults to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Object.is</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">hash</code></strong>: Custom hash function for change detection</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">sync</code></strong>: Whether to use synchronous updates (framework-specific)</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="accessing-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Accessing Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessing-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>In actions, guards, computed, and effects:</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">actions<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">increment</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> current <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">reset</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> initial <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">initial</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// Get initial value</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> initial<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">logName</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Current name:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<h3 id="how-bindable-works" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">How Bindable Works<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#how-bindable-works"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">bindable</code> pattern automatically:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Detects controlled vs uncontrolled state (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value !== undefined</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Manages framework-specific reactivity (React hooks, Solid signals, Vue refs,
Svelte runes)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Handles change notifications with equality checks</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Provides a consistent API across all frameworks</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="watch" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Watch<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#watch"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">watch</code> function allows you to reactively respond to changes in props or
context. It uses the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">track</code> function to specify dependencies and trigger
actions when they change.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token function">watch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> track<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action<span class="token punctuation">,</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// Track prop changes</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">track</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;enabled&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">action</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;updateEnabledState&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// Track context changes</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">track</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">action</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;logCount&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;updateDisplay&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// Track multiple dependencies</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">track</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;multiplier&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">action</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;calculateTotal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="how-track-works" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">How Track Works<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#how-track-works"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ol>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong>Dependency Array</strong>: Array of functions that return values to track</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong>Effect Function</strong>: Runs when any tracked dependency changes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong>Change Detection</strong>: Uses deep equality comparison (or custom <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isEqual</code> from
bindable)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong>Framework Integration</strong>: Each framework implements track using its
reactivity:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">React: <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useEffect</code> with dependency tracking</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Solid: <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">createEffect</code> with reactive signals</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Vue: <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">watch</code> with computed dependencies</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Svelte: Reactive statements</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="common-patterns" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Common Patterns<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#common-patterns"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Sync controlled props</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token function">watch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> track<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action<span class="token punctuation">,</span> prop <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">track</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;enabled&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">action</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;syncEnabledState&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// React to context changes</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token function">watch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> track<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">track</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">action</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;notifyCountChanged&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Track multiple values</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token function">watch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> track<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> prop <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">track</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;firstName&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;lastName&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">action</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;updateFullName&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="computed" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Computed<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#computed"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Computed values are derived from context, props, refs, and other computed
values. They&#x27;re recalculated whenever their dependencies change and are memoized
per framework.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">computed<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">isEven</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">%</span> <span class="token number">2</span> <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">0</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">fullName</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> first <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;firstName&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token string">&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> last <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;lastName&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token string">&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>first<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>last<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">trim</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// Computed can depend on other computed values</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">status</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> computed<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> isEven <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">computed</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;isEven&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> isEven <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Even: </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>count<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Odd: </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>count<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="accessing-computed" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Accessing Computed<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessing-computed"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// In guards</span>
</span><span class="code-line">guards<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">canIncrement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> computed <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token function">computed</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;isEven&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// Only increment when count is even</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// In actions</span>
</span><span class="code-line">actions<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">logStatus</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> computed <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> status <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">computed</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;status&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Status:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> status<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// In other computed values</span>
</span><span class="code-line">computed<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">message</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> computed <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token function">computed</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;isEven&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Count is even&quot;</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Count is odd&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="key-points" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Key Points<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#key-points"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Computed values are <strong>lazy</strong> - only calculated when accessed</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">They can depend on props, context, refs, scope, and other computed values</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">They&#x27;re <strong>memoized</strong> per framework (React <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMemo</code>, Solid <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">createMemo</code>, etc.)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Use computed for values that derive from state but don&#x27;t need to be stored in
context</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="refs" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Refs<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#refs"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Refs hold non-reactive references like class instances, DOM elements, or other
objects that don&#x27;t need reactivity. Unlike context, refs don&#x27;t trigger
re-renders when changed.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token function">refs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Simple counter for internal tracking</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    operationCount<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Cache for storing previous values</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    previousCount<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">null</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Simple object for tracking state</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    history<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="accessing-refs" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Accessing Refs<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessing-refs"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">actions<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">increment</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> refs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Store previous value in ref</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    refs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;previousCount&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> count<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Track operation</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> ops <span class="token operator">=</span> refs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;operationCount&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    refs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;operationCount&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> ops <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Update context</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> count <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">saveHistory</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> refs<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> history <span class="token operator">=</span> refs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;history&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    history<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">push</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>count<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    refs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;history&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> history<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="when-to-use-refs" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">When to Use Refs<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#when-to-use-refs"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Class instances that manage their own state</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Cached values that don&#x27;t need reactivity</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Temporary state that doesn&#x27;t affect rendering</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Performance-critical data that shouldn&#x27;t trigger updates</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="props" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Props<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Props are the configuration passed to your machine. The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">props</code> function
normalizes and sets defaults.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token function">props</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> props<span class="token punctuation">,</span> scope <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Set defaults</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    step<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    min<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    max<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Conditional defaults</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    enabled<span class="token operator">:</span> props<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">disabled</span> <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token keyword">undefined</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token operator">!</span>props<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Normalize values</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    initialValue<span class="token operator">:</span> props<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">initialValue</span> <span class="token operator">??</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Merge nested objects</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    settings<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      showLabel<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      showButtons<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token spread operator">...</span>props<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">settings</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// User props override defaults (spread last)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token spread operator">...</span>props<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="key-principles" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Key Principles<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#key-principles"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Always return defaults <strong>first</strong>, then spread <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">...props</code> to allow overrides</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Use conditional logic for interdependent defaults</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scope</code> parameter provides access to DOM scope (id, ids, getRootNode)</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="accessing-props" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Accessing Props<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessing-props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// In guards</span>
</span><span class="code-line">guards<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">canIncrement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> max <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;max&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> count <span class="token operator">&lt;</span> max
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// In actions</span>
</span><span class="code-line">actions<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">notifyChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;onChange&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">?.</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> count <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// In computed</span>
</span><span class="code-line">computed<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">canDecrement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> min <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;min&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> count <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> min
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="scope" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Scope<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#scope"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Scope provides access to DOM-related utilities and element queries. It&#x27;s
available in props, actions, guards, computed, and effects. Scope helps machines
interact with the DOM in a framework-agnostic way.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Scope interface</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">interface</span> <span class="token class-name">Scope</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  id<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">string</span> <span class="token comment">// Unique machine instance ID</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  ids<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">Record</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token builtin">string</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token builtin">any</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token comment">// Map of part IDs</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">getRootNode</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">ShadowRoot</span> <span class="token operator">|</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">Document</span> <span class="token operator">|</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">Node</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  getById<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token constant">T</span> <span class="token keyword">extends</span> <span class="token class-name">Element</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">HTMLElement</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">string</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token constant">T</span> <span class="token operator">|</span> <span class="token keyword">null</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">getActiveElement</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">HTMLElement</span> <span class="token operator">|</span> <span class="token keyword">null</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">isActiveElement</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>elem<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">HTMLElement</span> <span class="token operator">|</span> <span class="token keyword">null</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token builtin">boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">getDoc</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> <span class="token dom variable">document</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">getWin</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> <span class="token dom variable">window</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="using-scope" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Using Scope<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#using-scope"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Scope is commonly used in effects and actions to interact with DOM elements:</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">effects<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">focusInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> scope <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> inputEl <span class="token operator">=</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    inputEl<span class="token operator">?.</span><span class="token method function property-access">focus</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">trackClickOutside</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">,</span> send <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> doc <span class="token operator">=</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getDoc</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">handleClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>event<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">MouseEvent</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword">const</span> rootEl <span class="token operator">=</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getRootNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>rootEl<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">contains</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>event<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">target</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">Node</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token function">send</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> type<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;CLICK_OUTSIDE&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    doc<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">addEventListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;click&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> handleClick<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      doc<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">removeEventListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;click&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> handleClick<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="common-patterns-1" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Common Patterns<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#common-patterns-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get element by ID</span>
</span><span class="code-line">actions<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">scrollToElement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> scope <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> element <span class="token operator">=</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;target&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Check active element</span>
</span><span class="code-line">guards<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">isInputFocused</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> scope <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> inputEl <span class="token operator">=</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">isActiveElement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>inputEl<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Access document/window</span>
</span><span class="code-line">effects<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">preventScroll</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> scope <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> doc <span class="token operator">=</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getDoc</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> originalOverflow <span class="token operator">=</span> doc<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">body</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">style</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">overflow</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    doc<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">body</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">style</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">overflow</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">&quot;hidden&quot;</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      doc<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">body</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">style</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">overflow</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> originalOverflow
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
