</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Use in props for conditional defaults</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token function">props</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> props<span class="token punctuation">,</span> scope <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Use scope.id to generate unique IDs</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    id<span class="token operator">:</span> props<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">id</span> <span class="token operator">??</span> scope<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">id</span> <span class="token operator">??</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">counter-</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>Math<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">random</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token spread operator">...</span>props<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="key-points-1" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Key Points<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#key-points-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Scope provides framework-agnostic DOM access</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getById</code> to query elements by their generated IDs</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code> to get the root container (supports Shadow DOM)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getDoc</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getWin</code> for document/window access</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Scope is typically used in effects for DOM manipulation and event listeners</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="actions-guards-and-effects" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Actions, Guards, and Effects<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#actions-guards-and-effects"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>These are the implementation details that bring your machine to life.</p>
<h3 id="actions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Actions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#actions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Actions perform state updates and side effects:</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">actions<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">increment</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> prop <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> step <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;step&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> current <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> current <span class="token operator">+</span> step<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">notifyChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;onChange&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">?.</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> count <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">reset</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> initial <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">initial</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> initial<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="guards" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Guards<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#guards"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Guards are boolean conditions that determine if a transition should occur:</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">guards<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">canIncrement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> max <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;max&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> count <span class="token operator">&lt;</span> max
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">canDecrement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> min <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;min&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> count <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> min
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="effects" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Effects<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#effects"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Effects are side effects that run while in a state and must return cleanup:</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">effects<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">logCount</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> send <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Count changed to:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> count<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// No cleanup needed for this effect</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">undefined</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">startTimer</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> send <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> intervalId <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">setInterval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">send</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> type<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;TICK&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1000</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Return cleanup function</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">clearInterval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>intervalId<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><strong>Important</strong>: Effects must return a cleanup function (or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">undefined</code> if no
cleanup needed). Cleanup is called when exiting the state or unmounting.</p>
<h2 id="putting-it-all-together" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Putting It All Together<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#putting-it-all-together"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Here&#x27;s a complete example showing how these concepts work together in a simple
counter machine:</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">const</span> machine <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token generic-function"><span class="token function">createMachine</span><span class="token generic class-name"><span class="token operator">&lt;</span>CounterSchema<span class="token operator">&gt;</span></span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// 1. Normalize props</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">props</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> props <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      step<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      min<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      max<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      defaultValue<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token spread operator">...</span>props<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// 2. Define reactive context</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">context</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> bindable <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      count<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">bindable</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        defaultValue<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;defaultValue&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        value<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;value&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token function">onChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">          <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;onChange&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">?.</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> count<span class="token operator">:</span> value <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// 3. Define non-reactive refs</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">refs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// 4. Define computed values</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// 6. Define states and transitions</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  states<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    idle<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">decrement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> prop <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">        context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> current <span class="token operator">-</span> step<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">reset</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token keyword">const</span> initial <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">initial</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> initial<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">logCount</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> computed <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token keyword">const</span> isEven <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">computed</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;isEven&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Count: </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>count<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> (</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>isEven <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token string">&quot;even&quot;</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;odd&quot;</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">)</span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">notifyChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> context <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token keyword">const</span> count <span class="token operator">=</span> context<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;count&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;onChange&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">?.</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> count <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">logStepChanged</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> prop <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Step changed to:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token function">prop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;step&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="typescript-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">TypeScript Guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#typescript-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To make your machine type-safe, define a schema interface that describes all the
types:</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token keyword">type</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">EventObject</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">Machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">Service</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/core&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Define props interface</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token class-name"><span class="token keyword">export</span></span> <span class="token keyword">interface</span> <span class="token class-name">CounterProps</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  step<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  min<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  max<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  defaultValue<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  value<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  onChange<span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> count<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Define the machine schema</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">interface</span> <span class="token class-name">CounterSchema</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  state<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;idle&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  props<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">CounterProps</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  context<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    count<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  refs<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    previousCount<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span> <span class="token operator">|</span> <span class="token keyword">null</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    operationCount<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">number</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  computed<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    isEven<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    canIncrement<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    canDecrement<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  event<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">EventObject</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  action<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">string</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  guard<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">string</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  effect<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token builtin">string</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Create typed machine</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">const</span> machine <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token generic-function"><span class="token function">createMachine</span><span class="token generic class-name"><span class="token operator">&lt;</span>CounterSchema<span class="token operator">&gt;</span></span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ... machine definition</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Export typed service</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">export</span> <span class="token keyword">type</span> <span class="token class-name">CounterService</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token maybe-class-name">Service</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token maybe-class-name">CounterSchema</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="schema-properties" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Schema Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#schema-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">state</code></strong>: Union of all possible states (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;idle&quot; | &quot;active&quot; | &quot;disabled&quot;</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">props</code></strong>: Props interface (user configuration)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">context</code></strong>: Context values (reactive state)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">refs</code></strong>: Refs values (non-reactive references)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">computed</code></strong>: Computed values (derived state)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">event</code></strong>: Event types (usually <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">EventObject</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">action</code></strong>: Action names (usually <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">string</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">guard</code></strong>: Guard names (usually <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">string</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><strong><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">effect</code></strong>: Effect names (usually <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">string</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>This provides full type safety throughout your machine implementation.</p><a href="https://github.com/chakra-ui/zag/edit/main/website/data/guides/building-machines.mdx" class="d_inline-flex guide provides a deep dive into the key pieces that make Zag machines\nframework-agnostic and reactive.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eMachine Fundamentals\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eA state machine is a way to model stateful, reactive behavior using:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eA finite number of states\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eA finite number of transitions between those Machine\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eimport { createMachine } from \"@zag-js/core\"\n\ninterface ToggleSchema {\n  state: \"active\" | \"inactive\"\n  event: { type: \"CLICK\" }\n}\n\nexport const machine = createMachine\u0026#x3C;ToggleSchema\u003e({\n  initialState() {\n    return \"active\"\n  },\n  states: {\n    active: {\n      on: {\n        CLICK: { this guide explains the advanced building blocks used in production\nmachines.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eNested States\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eMachines can now model hierarchical state by nesting \u003ccode\u003estates\u003c/code\u003e inside a parent\nstate and defining the child's \u003ccode\u003einitial\u003c/code\u003e state.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eimport { createMachine } from \"@zag-js/core\"\n\nconst machine = createMachine({\n  initialState() {\n    return \"closed\"\n  },\n  states: {\n    closed: {\n      on: \"closed\" },\n      },\n    },\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eKey points:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse dot notation for nested targets, like \u003ccode\u003eopen.submitting\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eParent states can still define transitions (\u003ccode\u003eopen -\u003e CLOSE\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCheck nested activity with \u003ccode\u003eservice.state.matches(\"open.idle\")\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eContext\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eContext holds the reactive state of your machine. Unlike props (which are\nconfiguration), context represents internal state that changes over time.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eContext values are created using the \u003ccode\u003ebindable\u003c/code\u003e pattern, which provides\ncontrolled/uncontrolled state management.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econtext({ bindable, prop }) {\n  return {\n    // Uncontrolled state with default value\n    count: bindable\u0026#x3C;number\u003e(() =\u003e ({\n      defaultValue: 0,\n    })),\n\n    // Controlled/uncontrolled state\n    name: bindable\u0026#x3C;string\u003e(() =\u003e ({\n      defaultValue: prop(\"defaultName\") ?? \"\",\n      value: prop(\"name\"), // When provided, state is controlled\n      onChange(value, prev) {\n        prop(\"onNameChange\")?.({ name: value })\n      },\n    })),\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eBindable Parameters\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e: Initial value for uncontrolled state\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e: Controlled value from props (when provided, state becomes\ncontrolled)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonChange\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e: Callback fired when value changes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003eisEqual\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e: Custom equality function (defaults to \u003ccode\u003eObject.is\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003ehash\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e: Custom hash function for change detection\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003esync\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e: Whether to use synchronous updates (framework-specific)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAccessing Context\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn actions, guards, computed, and effects:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eactions: {\n  increment({ context }) {\n    const current = context.get(\"count\")\n    context.set(\"count\", current + 1) // Update context\n  },\n\n  reset({ context }) {\n    const initial = context.initial(\"count\") // Get initial value\n    context.set(\"count\", initial)\n  },\n\n  logName({ context }) {\n    const name = context.get(\"name\") // Read current value\n    console.log(\"Current name:\", name)\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eHow Bindable Works\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003ebindable\u003c/code\u003e pattern automatically:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDetects controlled vs uncontrolled state (\u003ccode\u003evalue !== undefined\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eManages framework-specific reactivity (React hooks, Solid signals, Vue refs,\nSvelte runes)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHandles change notifications with equality checks\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProvides a consistent API across all frameworks\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eWatch\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003ewatch\u003c/code\u003e function allows you to reactively respond to changes in props or\ncontext. It uses the \u003ccode\u003etrack\u003c/code\u003e function to specify dependencies and trigger\nactions when they change.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003ewatch({ track, action, prop, context }) {\n  // Track prop changes\n  track([() =\u003e prop(\"enabled\")], () =\u003e {\n    action([\"updateEnabledState\"])\n  })\n\n  // Track context changes\n  track([() =\u003e context.get(\"count\")], () =\u003e {\n    action([\"logCount\", \"updateDisplay\"])\n  })\n\n  // Track multiple dependencies\n  track([\n    () =\u003e context.get(\"count\"),\n    () =\u003e prop(\"multiplier\")\n  ], () =\u003e {\n    action([\"calculateTotal\"])\n  })\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eHow Track Works\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDependency Array\u003c/strong\u003e: Array of functions that return values to track\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEffect Function\u003c/strong\u003e: Runs when any tracked dependency changes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eChange Detection\u003c/strong\u003e: Uses deep equality comparison (or custom \u003ccode\u003eisEqual\u003c/code\u003e from\nbindable)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFramework Integration\u003c/strong\u003e: Each framework implements track using its\nreactivity:\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eReact: \u003ccode\u003euseEffect\u003c/code\u003e with dependency tracking\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSolid: \u003ccode\u003ecreateEffect\u003c/code\u003e with reactive signals\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eVue: \u003ccode\u003ewatch\u003c/code\u003e with computed dependencies\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSvelte: Reactive statements\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCommon Patterns\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003e// Sync controlled props\nwatch({ track, action, prop }) {\n  track([() =\u003e prop(\"enabled\")], () =\u003e {\n    action([\"syncEnabledState\"])\n  })\n}\n\n// React to context changes\nwatch({ track, action, context }) {\n  track([() =\u003e context.get(\"count\")], () =\u003e {\n    action([\"notifyCountChanged\"])\n  })\n}\n\n// Track multiple values\nwatch({ track, action, context, prop }) {\n  track([\n    () =\u003e context.get(\"firstName\"),\n    () =\u003e context.get(\"lastName\")\n  ], () =\u003e {\n    action([\"updateFullName\"])\n  })\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eComputed\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eComputed values are derived from context, props, refs, and other computed\nvalues. They're recalculated whenever their dependencies change and are memoized\nper framework.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003ecomputed: {\n  isEven({ context }) {\n    return context.get(\"count\") % 2 === 0\n  },\n\n  fullName({ context }) {\n    const first = context.get(\"firstName\") || \"\"\n    const last = context.get(\"lastName\") || \"\"\n    return `${first} ${last}`.trim()\n  },\n\n  // Computed can depend on other computed values\n  status({ computed, context }) {\n    const isEven = computed(\"isEven\")\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    return isEven ? `Even: ${count}` : `Odd: ${count}`\n  },\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAccessing Computed\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003e// In guards\nguards: {\n  canIncrement({ computed }) {\n    return computed(\"isEven\") // Only increment when count is even\n  }\n}\n\n// In actions\nactions: {\n  logStatus({ computed }) {\n    const status = computed(\"status\")\n    console.log(\"Status:\", status)\n  }\n}\n\n// In other computed values\ncomputed: {\n  message({ computed }) {\n    return computed(\"isEven\") ? \"Count is even\" : \"Count is odd\"\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eKey Points\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eComputed values are \u003cstrong\u003elazy\u003c/strong\u003e - only calculated when accessed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThey can depend on props, context, refs, scope, and other computed values\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThey're \u003cstrong\u003ememoized\u003c/strong\u003e per framework (React \u003ccode\u003euseMemo\u003c/code\u003e, Solid \u003ccode\u003ecreateMemo\u003c/code\u003e, etc.)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse computed for values that derive from state but don't need to be stored in\ncontext\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eRefs\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eRefs hold non-reactive references like class instances, DOM elements, or other\nobjects that don't need reactivity. Unlike context, refs don't trigger\nre-renders when changed.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003erefs() {\n  return {\n    // Simple counter for internal tracking\n    operationCount: 0,\n\n    // Cache for storing previous values\n    previousCount: null,\n\n    // Simple object for tracking state\n    history: [],\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAccessing Refs\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eactions: {\n  increment({ refs, context }) {\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n\n    // Store previous value in ref\n    refs.set(\"previousCount\", count)\n\n    // Track operation\n    const ops = refs.get(\"operationCount\")\n    refs.set(\"operationCount\", ops + 1)\n\n    // Update context\n    context.set(\"count\", count + 1)\n  },\n\n  saveHistory({ refs, context }) {\n    const history = refs.get(\"history\")\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    history.push(count)\n    refs.set(\"history\", history)\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eWhen to Use Refs\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eClass instances that manage their own state\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCached values that don't need reactivity\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTemporary state that doesn't affect rendering\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePerformance-critical data that shouldn't trigger updates\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eProps\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eProps are the configuration passed to your machine. The \u003ccode\u003eprops\u003c/code\u003e function\nnormalizes and sets defaults.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eprops({ props, scope }) {\n  return {\n    // Set defaults\n    step: 1,\n    min: 0,\n    max: 100,\n\n    // Conditional defaults\n    enabled: props.disabled === undefined ? true : !props.disabled,\n\n    // Normalize values\n    initialValue: props.initialValue ?? 0,\n\n    // Merge nested objects\n    settings: {\n      showLabel: true,\n      showButtons: true,\n      ...props.settings,\n    },\n\n    // User props override defaults (spread last)\n    ...props,\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eKey Principles\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAlways return defaults \u003cstrong\u003efirst\u003c/strong\u003e, then spread \u003ccode\u003e...props\u003c/code\u003e to allow overrides\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse conditional logic for interdependent defaults\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003escope\u003c/code\u003e parameter provides access to DOM scope (id, ids, getRootNode)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAccessing Props\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003e// In guards\nguards: {\n  canIncrement({ prop, context }) {\n    const max = prop(\"max\")\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    return count \u0026#x3C; max\n  }\n}\n\n// In actions\nactions: {\n  notifyChange({ prop, context }) {\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    prop(\"onChange\")?.({ count })\n  }\n}\n\n// In computed\ncomputed: {\n  canDecrement({ prop, context }) {\n    const min = prop(\"min\")\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    return count \u003e min\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eScope\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eScope provides access to DOM-related utilities and element queries. It's\navailable in props, actions, guards, computed, and effects. Scope helps machines\ninteract with the DOM in a framework-agnostic way.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003e// Scope interface\ninterface Scope {\n  id?: string // Unique machine instance ID\n  ids?: Record\u0026#x3C;string, any\u003e // Map of part IDs\n  getRootNode: () =\u003e ShadowRoot | Document | Node\n  getById: \u0026#x3C;T extends Element = HTMLElement\u003e(id: string) =\u003e T | null\n  getActiveElement: () =\u003e HTMLElement | null\n  isActiveElement: (elem: HTMLElement | null) =\u003e boolean\n  getDoc: () =\u003e typeof document\n  getWin: () =\u003e typeof window\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsing Scope\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eScope is commonly used in effects and actions to interact with DOM elements:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eeffects: {\n  focusInput({ scope }) {\n    const inputEl = scope.getById(\"input\")\n    inputEl?.focus()\n  },\n\n  trackClickOutside({ scope, send }) {\n    const doc = scope.getDoc()\n\n    function handleClick(event: MouseEvent) {\n      const rootEl = scope.getRootNode()\n      if (!rootEl.contains(event.target as Node)) {\n        send({ type: \"CLICK_OUTSIDE\" })\n      }\n    }\n\n    doc.addEventListener(\"click\", handleClick)\n    return () =\u003e {\n      doc.removeEventListener(\"click\", handleClick)\n    }\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCommon Patterns\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003e// Get element by ID\nactions: {\n  scrollToElement({ scope }) {\n    const element = scope.getById(\"target\")\n    element?.scrollIntoView()\n  }\n}\n\n// Check active element\nguards: {\n  isInputFocused({ scope }) {\n    const inputEl = scope.getById(\"input\")\n    return scope.isActiveElement(inputEl)\n  }\n}\n\n// Access document/window\neffects: {\n  preventScroll({ scope }) {\n    const doc = scope.getDoc()\n    const originalOverflow = doc.body.style.overflow\n    doc.body.style.overflow = \"hidden\"\n\n    return () =\u003e {\n      doc.body.style.overflow = originalOverflow\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n// Use in props for conditional defaults\nprops({ props, scope }) {\n  return {\n    // Use scope.id to generate unique IDs\n    id: props.id ?? scope.id ?? `counter-${Math.random()}`,\n    ...props,\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eKey Points\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eScope provides framework-agnostic DOM access\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003egetById\u003c/code\u003e to query elements by their generated IDs\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003egetRootNode\u003c/code\u003e to get the root container (supports Shadow DOM)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003egetDoc\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003egetWin\u003c/code\u003e for document/window access\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eScope is typically used in effects for DOM manipulation and event listeners\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eActions, Guards, and Effects\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThese are the implementation details that bring your machine to life.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eActions\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eActions perform state updates and side effects:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eactions: {\n  increment({ context, prop }) {\n    const step = prop(\"step\")\n    const current = context.get(\"count\")\n    context.set(\"count\", current + step)\n  },\n\n  notifyChange({ prop, context }) {\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    prop(\"onChange\")?.({ count })\n  },\n\n  reset({ context }) {\n    const initial = context.initial(\"count\")\n    context.set(\"count\", initial)\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eGuards\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eGuards are boolean conditions that determine if a transition should occur:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eguards: {\n  canIncrement({ prop, context }) {\n    const max = prop(\"max\")\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    return count \u0026#x3C; max\n  },\n\n  canDecrement({ prop, context }) {\n    const min = prop(\"min\")\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    return count \u003e min\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eEffects\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEffects are side effects that run while in a state and must return cleanup:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eeffects: {\n  logCount({ context, send }) {\n    const count = context.get(\"count\")\n    console.log(\"Count changed to:\", count)\n\n    // No cleanup needed for this effect\n    return undefined\n  },\n\n  startTimer({ send }) {\n    const intervalId = setInterval(() =\u003e {\n      send({ type: \"TICK\" })\n    }, 1000)\n\n    // Return cleanup function\n    return () =\u003e {\n      clearInterval(intervalId)\n    }\n  }\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImportant\u003c/strong\u003e: Effects must return a cleanup function (or \u003ccode\u003eundefined\u003c/code\u003e if no\ncleanup needed). Cleanup is called when exiting the state or unmounting.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003ePutting It All Together\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eHere's a complete example showing how these concepts work together in a simple\ncounter machine:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eexport const machine = createMachine\u0026#x3C;CounterSchema\u003e({\n  // 1. Normalize props\n  props({ props }) {\n    return {\n      step: 1,\n      min: 0,\n      max: 100,\n      defaultValue: 0,\n      ...props,\n    }\n  },\n\n  // 2. Define reactive context\n  context({ prop, bindable }) {\n    return {\n      count: bindable(() =\u003e ({\n        defaultValue: prop(\"defaultValue\"),\n        value: prop(\"value\"),\n        onChange(value) {\n          prop(\"onChange\")?.({ count: value })\n        },\n      })),\n    }\n  },\n\n  // 3. Define non-reactive refs\n  refs() {\n    return {\n      previousCount: null,\n      operationCount: 0,\n    }\n  },\n\n  // 4. Define computed values\n  computed: {\n    isEven({ context }) {\n      return context.get(\"count\") % 2 === 0\n    },\n    canIncrement({ prop, context }) {\n      const max = prop(\"max\")\n      const count = context.get(\"count\")\n      return count \u0026#x3C; max\n    },\n    canDecrement({ prop, context }) {\n      const min = prop(\"min\")\n      const count = context.get(\"count\")\n      return count \u003e min\n    },\n  },\n\n  // 5. Watch for changes\n  watch({ track, action, context, prop }) {\n    track([() =\u003e context.get(\"count\")], () =\u003e {\n      action([\"logCount\", \"notifyChange\"])\n    })\n    track([() =\u003e prop(\"step\")], () =\u003e {\n      action([\"logStepChanged\"])\n    })\n  },\n\n  // 6. Define states and transitions\n  states: {\n    idle: {\n      on: {\n        INCREMENT: {\n          guard: \"canIncrement\",\n          actions: [\"increment\"],\n        },\n        DECREMENT: {\n          guard: \"canDecrement\",\n          actions: [\"decrement\"],\n        },\n        RESET: {\n          actions: [\"reset\"],\n        },\n      },\n    },\n  },\n\n  // 7. Implement actions, guards, effects\n  implementations: {\n    guards: {\n      canIncrement({ computed }) {\n        return computed(\"canIncrement\")\n      },\n      canDecrement({ computed }) {\n        return computed(\"canDecrement\")\n      },\n    },\n    actions: {\n      increment({ context, prop, refs }) {\n        const step = prop(\"step\")\n        const current = context.get(\"count\")\n\n        // Store previous in ref\n        refs.set(\"previousCount\", current)\n\n        // Update context\n        context.set(\"count\", current + step)\n      },\n      decrement({ context, prop }) {\n        const step = prop(\"step\")\n        const current = context.get(\"count\")\n        context.set(\"count\", current - step)\n      },\n      reset({ context }) {\n        const initial = context.initial(\"count\")\n        context.set(\"count\", initial)\n      },\n      logCount({ context, computed }) {\n        const count = context.get(\"count\")\n        const isEven = computed(\"isEven\")\n        console.log(`Count: ${count} (${isEven ? \"even\" : \"odd\"})`)\n      },\n      notifyChange({ prop, context }) {\n        const count = context.get(\"count\")\n        prop(\"onChange\")?.({ count })\n      },\n      logStepChanged({ prop }) {\n        console.log(\"Step changed to:\", prop(\"step\"))\n      },\n    },\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eTypeScript Guide\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo make your machine type-safe, define a schema interface that describes all the\ntypes:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eimport type { EventObject, Machine, Service } from \"@zag-js/core\"\n\n// Define props interface\nexport interface
